 if ( (has_intersect(quickarray[selected_vganb_val], quickarray[29])) && (has_intersect(quickarray[selected_cpunb_val], quickarray[29])) && (has_intersect(quickarray[selected_typnb_val], quickarray[29])) )  		appendOptionLast('qs_preisnb', 'ab 1999 Euro', '29');

 	function has_intersect (arr1, arr2)  { 
 		var l1 = arr1.length, l2 = arr2.length, i, j, info;
 		for (i = 0; i < l1; i++)  { 
 			for (j = 0; j < l2; j++)  { 	
 				if (arr1[i] == arr2[j]) return true;
 			 } 
 		 } 
 		return false;
 	 } 
 	
 	
 	function appendOptionLast(selectid, optiontext, optionvalue)  { 
 		var elOptNew = document.createElement('option');
 		elOptNew.text = optiontext;
 		elOptNew.value = optionvalue;
 		var elSel = document.getElementById(selectid);
 
 		try  { 
 			elSel.add(elOptNew, null); // standards compliant; doesn't work in IE
 		 } 
 		catch(ex)  { 
 			elSel.add(elOptNew); // IE only
 		 } 
 	 } 
 
 	function selectByValue(selectid, optionvalue)  { 
 		var elSel = document.getElementById(selectid);
 		var i;
 		for (i = elSel.length - 1; i>=0; i--)  { 
 			if (elSel.options[i].value==optionvalue)  { 
 				elSel.options[i].selected = true;
 			 } 
 		 } 
 	 } 
 	
 	
 	function umschalten(wert)  { 
 				
 		if (wert=='pc')  { 
 		
 			document.getElementById("show_notebook").style.display = 'none';	
 			document.getElementById("show_pc").style.display = 'block';	
 					
 		 }  else  { 
 	
 			document.getElementById("show_pc").style.display = 'none';	
 			document.getElementById("show_notebook").style.display = 'block';	
 			
 		 } 
 	
 	 }
   </script>

         function showB2Binfo(zeigen) {
 	if (zeigen) {
 		document.getElementById("divB2Binfo").style.display='block';
 	} else {
 		document.getElementById("divB2Binfo").style.display='none';
 	}
 }
 
 function showB2Bchoose(zeigen) {
 	if (zeigen) {
 		document.getElementById("divB2Bchoose").style.display='block';
 	} else {
 		document.getElementById("divB2Bchoose").style.display='none';
 	}
 }
        </script>

    <script>
     function layover_umschalten(anschaltenId) {
 		
 		//alert(anschaltenId);
 
 		hochgezaehlt = 0;
 		document.getElementById("layover_pcsysteme").style.display="none";
 		document.getElementById("layover_pckomplett").style.display="none";
 		document.getElementById("layover_aufruestkits").style.display="none";
 		document.getElementById("layover_notebooks").style.display="none";
 		document.getElementById("layover_business").style.display="none";
 		document.getElementById("layover_peripherie").style.display="none";
 		document.getElementById("layover_gaming").style.display="none";
 		
 		if (anschaltenId.length > 0) 	{
 			document.getElementById(anschaltenId).style.display="inline-block";
 			// searchbar ausschalten
 			document.getElementById("searchbar").style.display="none";
 		} else {
 			// searchbar anschalten
 			document.getElementById("searchbar").style.display="block";
 		}
 	
 	}
    </script>

           <!-- Rahmen Anfang -->
           <script>
            function callAngebotTimer(duration) {
     var timer = duration;
     var days, hours, minutes, seconds;
     
     setInterval(function () {
 			
 				seconds = timer;
 				days = Math.floor(seconds / (3600*24));
 				seconds  -= days*3600*24;
 				hours   = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
 				seconds  -= hours*3600;
 				minutes = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
 				seconds  -= minutes*60;
 			
         //minutes = parseInt(timer / 60, 10)
         //seconds = parseInt(timer % 60, 10);
         
 				days 			= days < 10 ? "0" + days : days;	//>
 				hours 		= hours < 10 ? "0" + hours : hours;	//>
         minutes 	= minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;	//>
         seconds 	= seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;	//>
 
 				document.getElementById('daysAngebot').innerHTML = days;
 				document.getElementById('hoursAngebot').innerHTML = hours;
 				document.getElementById('minutesAngebot').innerHTML = minutes;
 				document.getElementById('secondsAngebot').innerHTML = seconds;
 
         if (--timer < 0) {	//>
             timer = 0;
         }
     }, 1000);
 }
 
 window.onload = function () {
 	
   callAngebotTimer(414000);
     
 };
           </script>

           function reiterWechseln(reiter) {
 	
 	scrollUntererSliderTo(1);
 	
 	if (reiter != 'topsellerSlider') {
 		document.getElementById('topsellerSlider').style.display = "none";
 		document.getElementById('topseller_img').src = "/templates/aganeu/img/aganeu/untenslider_topseller_aus.png";
 	}
 	
 	if (reiter != 'angeboteSlider') {
 		document.getElementById('angeboteSlider').style.display = "none";
 		document.getElementById('angebote_img').src = "/templates/aganeu/img/aganeu/untenslider_angebote_aus.png";
 	}
 	
 	if (reiter != 'neuigkeitenSlider') {
 		document.getElementById('neuigkeitenSlider').style.display = "none";
 		document.getElementById('neuigkeiten_img').src = "/templates/aganeu/img/aganeu/untenslider_neuigkeiten_aus.png";
 	}
 	
 	
 	
 	if (reiter == 'topsellerSlider') {
 		document.getElementById(reiter).style.display = "block";
 		document.getElementById('topseller_img').src = "/templates/aganeu/img/aganeu/untenslider_topseller_an.png";
 	}
 	
 	if (reiter == 'angeboteSlider') {
 		document.getElementById(reiter).style.display = "block";
 		document.getElementById('angebote_img').src = "/templates/aganeu/img/aganeu/untenslider_angebote_an.png";
 	}
 	
 	if (reiter == 'neuigkeitenSlider') {
 		document.getElementById(reiter).style.display = "block";
 		document.getElementById('neuigkeiten_img').src = "/templates/aganeu/img/aganeu/untenslider_neuigkeiten_an.png";
 	}
 	
 }
          </script>

           <script>
            function scrollUntererSliderTo(wohin) {
 	var scrollto = (wohin-1) * (240 * 4);
 	document.getElementById('btSlider1').style.backgroundColor = '#D4D4D4';
 	document.getElementById('btSlider2').style.backgroundColor = '#D4D4D4';
 	document.getElementById('btSlider3').style.backgroundColor = '#D4D4D4';
 	document.getElementById('btSlider4').style.backgroundColor = '#D4D4D4';
 	document.getElementById('btSlider'+wohin).style.backgroundColor = '#8B1919';
 	
 	$("#untererSlider").animate({ scrollLeft: scrollto }, 500);
 }
           </script>

                  Dass der AGANDO Konfigurator dabei
                  <strong>
                   fehlerresistent
                  </strong>
                  ist, also nur in sich schlüssige und technisch funktionierende Auswahlen zulässt, ist ein weiteres seiner herausragenden Merkmale gegenüber herkömmlichen Online-Konfiguratoren.
                 </td>
